<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">give me a list of 100 usefull linux commands</h1><a id="user-content-give-me-a-list-of-100-usefull-linux-commands" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: give me a list of 100 usefull linux commands" href="#give-me-a-list-of-100-usefull-linux-commands"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Here is a curated list of 100 useful Linux commands and concepts you can prepare for your Senior System Operations Engineer interview, covering file management, system monitoring, networking, user management, scripting, and troubleshooting. These commands align well with typical interview expectations for systems roles like yours:</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">File and Directory Management</h3><a id="user-content-file-and-directory-management" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: File and Directory Management" href="#file-and-directory-management"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><code>ls</code> – list files/directories</li>
<li><code>cd</code> – change directory</li>
<li><code>pwd</code> – print working directory</li>
<li><code>mkdir</code> – create directory</li>
<li><code>rmdir</code> – remove empty directory</li>
<li><code>rm</code> – remove files/directories</li>
<li><code>cp</code> – copy files/directories</li>
<li><code>mv</code> – move/rename files/directories</li>
<li><code>touch</code> – create empty file or update timestamp</li>
<li><code>find</code> – search files by criteria</li>
<li><code>locate</code> – find files by name quickly</li>
<li><code>stat</code> – show detailed file info</li>
<li><code>file</code> – determine file type</li>
<li><code>du</code> – disk usage of files/directories</li>
<li><code>df</code> – disk free space</li>
<li><code>tree</code> – display directory structure</li>
</ol>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">File Viewing and Text Processing</h3><a id="user-content-file-viewing-and-text-processing" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: File Viewing and Text Processing" href="#file-viewing-and-text-processing"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ol start="17" dir="auto">
<li><code>cat</code> – display file contents</li>
<li><code>less</code> / <code>more</code> – view file page-wise</li>
<li><code>head</code> – view first lines of file</li>
<li><code>tail</code> – view last lines of file (with <code>-f</code> for live logs)</li>
<li><code>grep</code> – search text patterns</li>
<li><code>awk</code> – text processing and reporting</li>
<li><code>sed</code> – stream editor for text manipulation</li>
<li><code>cut</code> – extract columns from text</li>
<li><code>sort</code> – sort lines</li>
<li><code>uniq</code> – filter duplicate lines</li>
<li><code>wc</code> – word/line/character count</li>
<li><code>tr</code> – translate or delete characters</li>
</ol>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Permissions and Ownership</h3><a id="user-content-permissions-and-ownership" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Permissions and Ownership" href="#permissions-and-ownership"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ol start="29" dir="auto">
<li><code>chmod</code> – change file permissions</li>
<li><code>chown</code> – change file owner/group</li>
<li><code>umask</code> – set default permission mask</li>
<li><code>getfacl</code> / <code>setfacl</code> – manage Access Control Lists</li>
</ol>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Process Management</h3><a id="user-content-process-management" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Process Management" href="#process-management"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ol start="33" dir="auto">
<li><code>ps</code> – list running processes</li>
<li><code>top</code> / <code>htop</code> – interactive process viewer</li>
<li><code>kill</code> – terminate process by PID</li>
<li><code>killall</code> – terminate process by name</li>
<li><code>nice</code> / <code>renice</code> – set/change process priority</li>
<li><code>jobs</code> – list background jobs</li>
<li><code>fg</code> / <code>bg</code> – foreground/background jobs</li>
<li><code>pstree</code> – display process tree</li>
</ol>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">System Monitoring and Logs</h3><a id="user-content-system-monitoring-and-logs" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: System Monitoring and Logs" href="#system-monitoring-and-logs"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ol start="41" dir="auto">
<li><code>uptime</code> – system uptime and load</li>
<li><code>vmstat</code> – virtual memory stats</li>
<li><code>iostat</code> – CPU and I/O stats</li>
<li><code>free</code> – memory usage</li>
<li><code>sar</code> – system activity report</li>
<li><code>dmesg</code> – kernel ring buffer logs</li>
<li><code>journalctl</code> – systemd logs</li>
<li><code>tail -f /var/log/syslog</code> – live system logs</li>
<li><code>netstat</code> / <code>ss</code> – network connections and stats</li>
<li><code>lsof</code> – list open files</li>
</ol>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Networking</h3><a id="user-content-networking" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Networking" href="#networking"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ol start="51" dir="auto">
<li><code>ping</code> – test connectivity</li>
<li><code>traceroute</code> – trace network path</li>
<li><code>nslookup</code> / <code>dig</code> – DNS queries</li>
<li><code>ifconfig</code> / <code>ip</code> – network interface config</li>
<li><code>route</code> – show routing table</li>
<li><code>tcpdump</code> – packet capture</li>
<li><code>wget</code> / <code>curl</code> – download files or test HTTP</li>
<li><code>ssh</code> – remote login</li>
<li><code>scp</code> / <code>rsync</code> – secure copy/sync files</li>
<li><code>netcat</code> (nc) – network utility for debugging</li>
</ol>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Package and Service Management</h3><a id="user-content-package-and-service-management" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Package and Service Management" href="#package-and-service-management"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ol start="61" dir="auto">
<li><code>yum</code> / <code>dnf</code> / <code>apt</code> – package management</li>
<li><code>rpm</code> / <code>dpkg</code> – package query/install</li>
<li><code>systemctl</code> – manage systemd services</li>
<li><code>service</code> – start/stop services (SysV init)</li>
<li><code>chkconfig</code> – configure service startup</li>
<li><code>cron</code> / <code>crontab</code> – schedule jobs</li>
</ol>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Disk and Storage</h3><a id="user-content-disk-and-storage" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Disk and Storage" href="#disk-and-storage"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ol start="67" dir="auto">
<li><code>mount</code> / <code>umount</code> – mount/unmount filesystems</li>
<li><code>lsblk</code> – list block devices</li>
<li><code>fdisk</code> / <code>parted</code> – disk partitioning</li>
<li><code>df</code> – disk free space</li>
<li><code>tune2fs</code> – adjust ext2/ext3/ext4 filesystem parameters</li>
<li><code>fsck</code> – filesystem check and repair</li>
<li><code>lvm</code> – manage Logical Volume Manager</li>
<li><code>blkid</code> – display block device attributes</li>
</ol>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">User and Group Management</h3><a id="user-content-user-and-group-management" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: User and Group Management" href="#user-and-group-management"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ol start="75" dir="auto">
<li><code>id</code> – show user ID and groups</li>
<li><code>who</code> / <code>w</code> – who is logged in</li>
<li><code>users</code> – list logged-in users</li>
<li><code>useradd</code> / <code>adduser</code> – add user</li>
<li><code>usermod</code> – modify user</li>
<li><code>passwd</code> – change user password</li>
<li><code>groupadd</code> / <code>groupmod</code> – manage groups</li>
<li><code>sudo</code> – run commands as root</li>
<li><code>su</code> – switch user</li>
</ol>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Scripting and Automation</h3><a id="user-content-scripting-and-automation" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Scripting and Automation" href="#scripting-and-automation"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ol start="84" dir="auto">
<li><code>bash</code> / <code>sh</code> – shell scripting</li>
<li><code>cron</code> – schedule scripts/jobs</li>
<li><code>at</code> – schedule one-time jobs</li>
<li><code>env</code> – show environment variables</li>
<li><code>export</code> – set environment variables</li>
<li><code>alias</code> – create command shortcuts</li>
<li><code>xargs</code> – build argument lists from input</li>
</ol>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">System Information and Configuration</h3><a id="user-content-system-information-and-configuration" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: System Information and Configuration" href="#system-information-and-configuration"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ol start="91" dir="auto">
<li><code>uname</code> – system info</li>
<li><code>hostname</code> – show/set hostname</li>
<li><code>uptime</code> – system uptime</li>
<li><code>date</code> – show/set date and time</li>
<li><code>timedatectl</code> – manage time settings</li>
<li><code>free</code> – memory usage</li>
<li><code>lsmod</code> – list loaded kernel modules</li>
<li><code>modprobe</code> – add/remove kernel modules</li>
<li><code>sysctl</code> – modify kernel parameters</li>
<li><code>strace</code> – trace system calls of a process</li>
</ol>
<hr>
<p dir="auto">This list covers commands you can expect to use or be asked about in a systems operations role, especially one involving Linux system support, monitoring, automation, and troubleshooting<sup><a href="#user-content-fn-1-d94d5d61a147eb6ff64d790dd318b2c5" id="user-content-fnref-1-d94d5d61a147eb6ff64d790dd318b2c5" data-footnote-ref="" aria-describedby="footnote-label">1</a></sup><sup><a href="#user-content-fn-2-d94d5d61a147eb6ff64d790dd318b2c5" id="user-content-fnref-2-d94d5d61a147eb6ff64d790dd318b2c5" data-footnote-ref="" aria-describedby="footnote-label">2</a></sup><sup><a href="#user-content-fn-3-d94d5d61a147eb6ff64d790dd318b2c5" id="user-content-fnref-3-d94d5d61a147eb6ff64d790dd318b2c5" data-footnote-ref="" aria-describedby="footnote-label">3</a></sup><sup><a href="#user-content-fn-7-d94d5d61a147eb6ff64d790dd318b2c5" id="user-content-fnref-7-d94d5d61a147eb6ff64d790dd318b2c5" data-footnote-ref="" aria-describedby="footnote-label">4</a></sup><sup><a href="#user-content-fn-8-d94d5d61a147eb6ff64d790dd318b2c5" id="user-content-fnref-8-d94d5d61a147eb6ff64d790dd318b2c5" data-footnote-ref="" aria-describedby="footnote-label">5</a></sup>.</p>
